5:T196ca,<h2 id="문자열-리터럴-string-literal"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#문자열-리터럴-string-literal">문자열 리터럴 (String Literal)</a></h2>
<p>문자열 리터럴은 소스 코드에 직접 작성된 문자열입니다. 예: <code>"Hello, World!"</code></p>
<h3 id="특징"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#특징">특징</a></h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>읽기 전용 메모리</strong>에 저장 (일반적으로 코드 세그먼트)</li>
<li><strong>수정 불가능</strong> (수정 시도 시 정의되지 않은 동작)</li>
<li>프로그램 실행 중 <strong>메모리 주소가 고정</strong>됨</li>
<li>같은 리터럴은 <strong>메모리를 공유</strong>할 수 있음</li>
</ol>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> *</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">str1 </span><span style="color:#86E1FC">=</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 같은 리터럴이면 같은 주소를 가리킬 수 있음</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%p</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 예: 0x4005f4</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%p</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str2</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 예: 0x4005f4 (같은 주소)</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 수정 시도 - 위험! (정의되지 않은 동작)</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // str1[0] = 'h';  // 런타임 에러 가능</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    return</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">}</span></span><button type="button" title="Copy code" aria-label="Copy code" data="#include <stdio.h>

int main() {
    // 문자열 리터럴을 포인터에 할당
    char *str1 = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    char *str2 = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    // 같은 리터럴이면 같은 주소를 가리킬 수 있음

<h2 id="문자열-배열-string-array"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#문자열-배열-string-array">문자열 배열 (String Array)</a></h2>
<p>문자열 배열은 스택에 할당되는 수정 가능한 문자열입니다.</p>
<h3 id="특징-1"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#특징-1">특징</a></h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>스택 메모리</strong>에 저장</li>
<li><strong>수정 가능</strong></li>
<li>함수 종료 시 <strong>자동으로 해제</strong>됨</li>
<li>각 배열은 <strong>독립적인 메모리</strong> 공간을 가짐</li>
</ol>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">string.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 문자열 배열 선언 방법들</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 방법 1: 크기 명시</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">20</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 방법 2: 자동 크기 결정</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str2</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 크기는 6 (NULL 문자 포함)</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> str3</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">20</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">];</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    strcpy</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">str3</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 수정 가능</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#C8D3F5">    str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> '</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">'</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%s</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "hello"</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 각 배열은 독립적인 메모리</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%p</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 서로 다른 주소</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%p</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str2</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 서로 다른 주소</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    return</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>

#include <string.h>

int main() {
    // 문자열 배열 선언 방법들

    // 방법 1: 크기 명시
    char str1[20] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    // 방법 2: 자동 크기 결정
    char str2[] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;  // 크기는 6 (NULL 문자 포함)

    // 방법 3: 초기화 후 나중에 할당
    char str3[20];
    strcpy(str3, &#x22;Hello&#x22;);

    // 수정 가능
    str1[0] = &#x27;h&#x27;;
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, str1);  // &#x22;hello&#x22;

    // 각 배열은 독립적인 메모리
    printf(&#x22;%p\n&#x22;, str1);  // 서로 다른 주소
    printf(&#x22;%p\n&#x22;, str2);  // 서로 다른 주소

    return 0;

<h2 id="문자열-포인터-vs-문자열-배열"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#문자열-포인터-vs-문자열-배열">문자열 포인터 vs 문자열 배열</a></h2>

<ul>
<li>포인터 변수는 스택에 저장</li>

int main() {
    // 문자열 리터럴 (읽기 전용 메모리, 보통 코드 세그먼트)
    char *literal1 = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    char *literal2 = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    // 문자열 배열 (스택 메모리)
    char arr1[] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    char arr2[] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    printf(&#x22;리터럴 주소:\n&#x22;);
    printf(&#x22;literal1: %p\n&#x22;, literal1);
    printf(&#x22;literal2: %p\n&#x22;, literal2);
    // 같은 리터럴이면 같은 주소일 수 있음

    printf(&#x22;\n배열 주소:\n&#x22;);
    printf(&#x22;arr1: %p\n&#x22;, arr1);
    printf(&#x22;arr2: %p\n&#x22;, arr2);
    // 각 배열은 독립적인 메모리 (다른 주소)

    return 0;

<h2 id="sizeof-연산자-차이"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#sizeof-연산자-차이">sizeof 연산자 차이</a></h2>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> *</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">ptr </span><span style="color:#86E1FC">=</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> arr</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 포인터의 크기 (포인터 변수 자체의 크기)</span></span>

int main() {
    // 문자열 포인터 (읽기 전용)

    // 배열은 수정 가능
    arr[0] = &#x27;h&#x27;;
    strcpy(arr, &#x22;World&#x22;);  // 가능
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, arr);  // &#x22;World&#x22;

    // 포인터는 수정 불가

    // arr = &#x22;World&#x22;;  // 컴파일 에러

    return 0;

    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, str);
    // str[0] = &#x27;X&#x27;;  // 위험! (리터럴이면 수정 불가)

    char *ptr = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    return 0;

<h3 id="배열로-전달-실제로는-포인터로-변환됨"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#배열로-전달-실제로는-포인터로-변환됨">배열로 전달 (실제로는 포인터로 변환됨)</a></h3>

#include <string.h>

void modify_string(char *str) {
    // str이 리터럴인지 배열인지 확인 불가
    // 안전하게 수정하려면 배열을 전달해야 함

    // 방법 1: 새로운 배열 생성
    char buffer[100];
    strcpy(buffer, str);
    buffer[0] = &#x27;X&#x27;;  // 안전
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, buffer);
}

int main() {
    char *literal = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    char arr[] = &#x22;World&#x22;;

    // 리터럴을 수정하려고 하면 위험
    modify_string(literal);  // 내부에서 복사하므로 안전

    // 배열은 안전
    modify_string(arr);

    return 0;

<h3 id="const-키워드-사용"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#const-키워드-사용">const 키워드 사용</a></h3>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>

#include <stdlib.h>

int main() {
    char *literal = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;

    // 방법 1: 배열로 복사 (스택)
    char arr[20];
    strcpy(arr, literal);
    arr[0] = &#x27;h&#x27;;  // 안전하게 수정 가능
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, arr);

    // 방법 2: 동적 할당으로 복사 (힙)
    char *dynamic = (char *)malloc(strlen(literal) + 1);
    strcpy(dynamic, literal);
    dynamic[0] = &#x27;h&#x27;;  // 안전하게 수정 가능
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, dynamic);
    free(dynamic);

    return 0;

<h3 id="3-sizeof와-strlen-혼동"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#3-sizeof와-strlen-혼동">3. sizeof와 strlen 혼동</a></h3>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">char</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> arr</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>

<h2 id="요약-표"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#요약-표">요약 표</a></h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>구분</th>
<th>문자열 리터럴 (포인터)</th>
<th>문자열 배열</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>선언</td>
<td><code>char *str = "Hello"</code></td>
<td><code>char str[] = "Hello"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>메모리 위치</td>
<td>읽기 전용 메모리 (코드 세그먼트)</td>
<td>스택 메모리</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>수정 가능</td>
<td>❌ 불가능</td>
<td>✅ 가능</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>sizeof 결과</td>
<td>포인터 크기 (8 또는 4)</td>
<td>배열 크기 (문자열 길이 + 1)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>재할당</td>
<td>✅ 가능 (다른 리터럴 가리키기)</td>
<td>❌ 불가능</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>메모리 공유</td>
<td>같은 리터럴은 공유 가능</td>
<td>각각 독립적</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>함수 매개변수</td>
<td>포인터로 전달</td>
<td>포인터로 변환되어 전달</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 id="실전-팁"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#실전-팁">실전 팁</a></h2>
<ol>
<li><strong>수정이 필요하면 배열 사용</strong>: <code>char arr[] = "Hello"</code></li>
<li><strong>읽기만 하면 포인터 사용</strong>: <code>const char *str = "Hello"</code></li>
<li><strong>함수 매개변수는 포인터 사용</strong>: 배열도 자동으로 포인터로 변환됨</li>
<li><strong>동적 할당은 필요할 때만</strong>: <code>malloc()</code> 사용 후 반드시 <code>free()</code></li>
<li><strong>const 키워드 적극 활용</strong>: 의도를 명확히 하고 실수 방지</li>

a:T30839,<h2 id="메모리-함수-stringh"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#메모리-함수-stringh">메모리 함수 (string.h)</a></h2>
<h3 id="memcpy---메모리-복사"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#memcpy---메모리-복사">memcpy - 메모리 복사</a></h3>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">string.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>

<ul>
<li><code>src</code>에서 <code>dest</code>로 <code>n</code> 바이트를 복사</li>
<li>메모리 영역이 겹치면 정의되지 않은 동작 (겹치면 <code>memmove</code> 사용)</li>
<li>반환값: <code>dest</code> 포인터</li>
</ul>

#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char src[] = &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;;
    char dest[20];

    memcpy(dest, src, strlen(src) + 1);  // +1은 NULL 문자 포함
    printf(&#x22;복사된 문자열: %s\n&#x22;, dest);  // &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;

    // 배열 복사
    int arr1[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};
    int arr2[5];
    memcpy(arr2, arr1, sizeof(arr1));

    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
        printf(&#x22;%d &#x22;, arr2[i]);  // 1 2 3 4 5
    }
    return 0;

<ul>
<li><code>memcpy</code>와 동일하지만 메모리 영역이 겹쳐도 안전</li>
<li>반환값: <code>dest</code> 포인터</li>
</ul>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello, World!</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    memmove</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">str</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str </span><span style="color:#86E1FC">+</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 7</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 6</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "World!"를 앞으로 이동</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#C8D3F5">    str</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">6</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> '\0'</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%s</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "World!"</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">}</span></span><button type="button" title="Copy code" aria-label="Copy code" data="#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char str[] = &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;;

    // 메모리가 겹치는 경우 (str[7]부터 str[0]으로 복사)
    memmove(str, str + 7, 6);  // &#x22;World!&#x22;를 앞으로 이동
    str[6] = &#x27;\0&#x27;;
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, str);  // &#x22;World!&#x22;

    // 배열 요소 이동
    int arr[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};
    memmove(arr + 1, arr, 4 * sizeof(int));  // 한 칸씩 오른쪽으로
    arr[0] = 0;
    // 결과: {0, 1, 2, 3, 4}

    return 0;

<ul>
<li>메모리 영역을 특정 값으로 초기화</li>
<li><code>c</code>는 <code>unsigned char</code>로 변환되어 사용</li>
<li>반환값: <code>s</code> 포인터</li>
</ul>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">string.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">100</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">];</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 0으로 초기화</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    memset</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> sizeof(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">));</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 특정 문자로 채우기</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    memset</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> '</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">A</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">'</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 10</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#C8D3F5">    buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">10</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> '\0'</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%s</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> buffer</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "AAAAAAAAAA"</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 배열 초기화</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    int</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> arr</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">10</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">];</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    memset</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">arr</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> sizeof(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">arr</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">));</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 모든 요소를 0으로</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // -1로 초기화 (주의: int는 4바이트이므로 0xFFFFFFFF가 됨)</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    memset</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">arr</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> -</span><span style="color:#FF966C">1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> sizeof(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">arr</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">));</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    return</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">}</span></span><button type="button" title="Copy code" aria-label="Copy code" data="#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char buffer[100];

    // 0으로 초기화
    memset(buffer, 0, sizeof(buffer));

    // 특정 문자로 채우기
    memset(buffer, &#x27;A&#x27;, 10);
    buffer[10] = &#x27;\0&#x27;;
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, buffer);  // &#x22;AAAAAAAAAA&#x22;

    // 배열 초기화
    int arr[10];
    memset(arr, 0, sizeof(arr));  // 모든 요소를 0으로

    // -1로 초기화 (주의: int는 4바이트이므로 0xFFFFFFFF가 됨)
    memset(arr, -1, sizeof(arr));

    return 0;

<h3 id="memcmp---메모리-비교"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#memcmp---메모리-비교">memcmp - 메모리 비교</a></h3>

<ul>
<li>두 메모리 영역을 바이트 단위로 비교</li>
<li>반환값:
<ul>
<li><code>s1 &#x3C; s2</code>: 음수</li>
<li><code>s1 == s2</code>: 0</li>
<li><code>s1 > s2</code>: 양수</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">string.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str1</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str2</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str3</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">World</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 문자열 비교</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    int</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> result1 </span><span style="color:#86E1FC">=</span><span style="color:#65BCFF"> memcmp</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">str1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str2</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 5</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%d</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> result1</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // 0 (같음)</span></span>

#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char str[] = &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;;

    // &#x27;W&#x27; 문자 찾기
    char *found = (char *)memchr(str, &#x27;W&#x27;, strlen(str));
    if (found) {
        printf(&#x22;찾음: %s\n&#x22;, found);  // &#x22;World!&#x22;

    // 배열에서 특정 값 찾기
    int arr[] = {10, 20, 30, 40, 50};
    int *ptr = (int *)memchr(arr, 30, sizeof(arr));
    if (ptr) {
        printf(&#x22;값 30을 찾았습니다: 인덱스 %ld\n&#x22;, ptr - arr);
    }

    return 0;

<h3 id="strlen---문자열-길이"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#strlen---문자열-길이">strlen - 문자열 길이</a></h3>

<ul>
<li>최대 <code>n</code> 문자까지 복사</li>
<li><code>n</code>이 <code>src</code> 길이보다 크면 나머지는 NULL 문자로 채움</li>
<li>반환값: <code>dest</code> 포인터</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><code>src</code>에서 최대 <code>n</code> 문자를 <code>dest</code> 끝에 연결</li>
<li>자동으로 NULL 문자 추가</li>
<li>반환값: <code>dest</code> 포인터</li>
</ul>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">string.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5"> dest</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">[</span><span style="color:#FF966C">50</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">Hello</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> src</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">, World!</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    strncat</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">dest</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> src</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 3</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // ", W"만 추가</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    printf</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">%s</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">\n"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> dest</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "Hello, W"</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    return</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">}</span></span><button type="button" title="Copy code" aria-label="Copy code" data="#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char dest[50] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    char src[] = &#x22;, World!&#x22;;

    strncat(dest, src, 3);  // &#x22;, W&#x22;만 추가

<ul>
<li>두 문자열을 사전식으로 비교</li>
<li>반환값:
<ul>
<li><code>s1 &#x3C; s2</code>: 음수</li>
<li><code>s1 == s2</code>: 0</li>
<li><code>s1 > s2</code>: 양수</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

#include <string.h>

int main() {
    char str[] = &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;;

    char *found = strchr(str, &#x27;o&#x27;);
    if (found) {
        printf(&#x22;찾음: %s\n&#x22;, found);  // &#x22;o, World!&#x22;
        printf(&#x22;인덱스: %ld\n&#x22;, found - str);  // 4
    }

    // 모든 &#x27;o&#x27; 찾기
    char *ptr = str;
    while ((ptr = strchr(ptr, &#x27;o&#x27;)) != NULL) {
        printf(&#x22;위치: %ld\n&#x22;, ptr - str);
        ptr++;  // 다음 위치부터 검색
    }

    return 0;

<ul>
<li>문자열을 구분자로 분리</li>
<li>첫 번째 호출: <code>str</code> 전달</li>
<li>이후 호출: NULL 전달 (이전 문자열 계속 사용)</li>
<li>반환값: 토큰 포인터, 더 이상 없으면 NULL</li>
</ul>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">#include</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">stdio.h</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">></span></span>

<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0"> str</span><span style="color:#C099FF">[]</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">apple,banana,cherry</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">    char</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> *</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">token</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // 첫 번째 토큰</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#B4C2F0">    token </span><span style="color:#86E1FC">=</span><span style="color:#65BCFF"> strtok</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#B4C2F0">str</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> "</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">,</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    }</span></span>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // apple</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // banana</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">    // cherry</span></span>

<h2 id="안전한-함수-c11"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#안전한-함수-c11">안전한 함수 (C11)</a></h2>
<h3 id="strcpy_s-strcat_s-등"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#strcpy_s-strcat_s-등">strcpy_s, strcat_s 등</a></h3>
<p>C11 표준에서는 더 안전한 함수들이 추가되었습니다 (일부 컴파일러에서만 지원).</p>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="c" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">// 예시 (Microsoft Visual C++ 등)</span></span>

<h2 id="주의사항"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#주의사항">주의사항</a></h2>
<ol>
<li><strong>버퍼 오버플로우</strong>: <code>strcpy</code>, <code>strcat</code> 등은 버퍼 크기를 확인하지 않음</li>
<li><strong>NULL 포인터</strong>: 모든 함수는 유효한 포인터를 받아야 함</li>
<li><strong>메모리 겹침</strong>: <code>memcpy</code>는 메모리가 겹치면 안 됨 (겹치면 <code>memmove</code> 사용)</li>
<li><strong>NULL 문자</strong>: 문자열 함수는 NULL 문자(<code>\0</code>)를 기준으로 동작</li>
<li><strong>strtok의 재진입 불가</strong>: <code>strtok</code>는 내부 정적 변수를 사용하므로 스레드 안전하지 않음</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="실전-예제"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#실전-예제">실전 예제</a></h2>

#include <string.h>

void reverse_string(char *str) {
    int len = strlen(str);
    for (int i = 0; i < len / 2; i++) {
        char temp = str[i];
        str[i] = str[len - 1 - i];
        str[len - 1 - i] = temp;
    }
}

int main() {
    char str[] = &#x22;Hello&#x22;;
    reverse_string(str);
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, str);  // &#x22;olleH&#x22;
    return 0;

<h3 id="문자열에서-숫자-추출"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#문자열에서-숫자-추출">문자열에서 숫자 추출</a></h3>

<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    }</span></span>

<span data-line=""> </span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#FFC777">int</span><span style="color:#82AAFF"> main</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">()</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> {</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#65BCFF">    extract_numbers</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">(</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">abc123def456</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">"</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">);</span><span style="color:#858AA6">  // "123456"</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">    return</span><span style="color:#FF966C"> 0</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#86E1FC">}</span></span><button type="button" title="Copy code" aria-label="Copy code" data="#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <ctype.h>

void extract_numbers(const char *str) {
    while (*str) {
        if (isdigit(*str)) {
            printf(&#x22;%c&#x22;, *str);
        }
        str++;
    }
    printf(&#x22;\n&#x22;);
}

int main() {
    extract_numbers(&#x22;abc123def456&#x22;);  // &#x22;123456&#x22;
    return 0;

#include <string.h>

void safe_strcpy(char *dest, size_t dest_size, const char *src) {
    if (dest == NULL || src == NULL || dest_size == 0) {
        return;
    }

    size_t src_len = strlen(src);
    size_t copy_len = (src_len < dest_size - 1) ? src_len : dest_size - 1;

    memcpy(dest, src, copy_len);
    dest[copy_len] = &#x27;\0&#x27;;
}

int main() {
    char dest[10];
    safe_strcpy(dest, sizeof(dest), &#x22;Hello, World!&#x22;);
    printf(&#x22;%s\n&#x22;, dest);  // &#x22;Hello, Wo&#x22; (안전하게 잘림)
    return 0;
